Per-Request Filter Instantiation\\nThe `FilterChainManager` interface (envoy/http/filter_factory.h:70) is implemented by `FilterManager` (source/common/http/filter_manager.h:638):\\n\\n- `FilterManager::applyFilterFactoryCb()` (source/common/http/filter_manager.cc:551) creates a temporary `FilterChainFactoryCallbacksImpl` object\\n- It invokes the filter factory callback: `factory(callbacks)` - this is where the actual filter instance is created\\n- The callback typically calls `callbacks.addStreamDecoderFilter()` to instantiate the filter\\n- In `FilterChainFactoryCallbacksImpl::addStreamDecoderFilter()` (source/common/http/filter_manager.h:918-922), the filter is wrapped in an `ActiveStreamDecoderFilter` and added to the decoder_filters_ list for this stream\\n\\nThis design separates factory registration (static, at startup) from filter instantiation (dynamic, per-request), allowing factory methods to be simple pure virtual functions that return configured callbacks, which are then invoked to create actual filter instances when needed.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
